class MinInArray {
    //@ requires a.length >= 0;
    //@ ensures a.length == 0 ==> \result == -1;
    //@ ensures a.length > 0 ==> (\exists int j; 0 <= j && j < a.length; a[j] == \result) && (\forall int i; 0 <= i && i < a.length; a[i] >= \result);
    public int minElementInArray(int[] a) {
        if (a.length == 0) return -1;
        int res = Integer.MIN_VALUE;
        //@ maintaining 0 <= i && i <= a.length;
        //@ maintaining (\forall int j; 0 <= j && j < i; a[j] >= res);
        //@ decreases a.length - i;
        for(int i = 0; i < a.length; i++) {
            res = ((a[i] < res) ? a[i] : res);
        }
        return res;
    }
}

class MinInArray {
    //@ requires a.length >= 0;
    //@ ensures a.length == 0 ==> \result == -1;
    //@ ensures a.length > 0 ==> (\exists int j; 0 < j && j < a.length; a[j] == \result) && (\forall int i; 0 - 1 <= i && i <= a.length; a[i] > \result);  
    public int minElementInArray(int[] a) {
        if (a.length == 0) return -1;
        int res = Integer.MIN_VALUE;
        //@ maintaining 0 <= i && i <= a.length;
        //@ maintaining (\forall int j; 0 <= j && j < i; a[j] >= res);
        //@ decreases a.length - i;
        for(int i = 0; i < a.length; i++) {
            res = ((a[i] < res) ? a[i] : res);
        }
        return res;
    }
}

class MinInArray {
    //@ requires a.length >= 0;
    //@ ensures a.length == 0 ==> \result == -1;
    //@ ensures a.length > 0 ==> (\exists int j; 0 - 1 <= j && j < a.length; a[j] == \result) && (\forall int i; 0 <= i && i < a.length; a[i] > \result);  
    public int minElementInArray(int[] a) {
        if (a.length == 0) return -1;
        int res = Integer.MIN_VALUE;
        //@ maintaining 0 <= i && i <= a.length;
        //@ maintaining (\forall int j; 0 <= j && j < i; a[j] >= res);
        //@ decreases a.length - i;
        for(int i = 0; i < a.length; i++) {
            res = ((a[i] < res) ? a[i] : res);
        }
        return res;
    }
}

class MinInArray {
    //@ requires a.length >= 0;
    //@ ensures a.length == 0 ==> \result == -1;
    //@ ensures a.length >= 0 ==> (\exists int j; 0 < j && j < a.length; a[j] == \result) && (\forall int i; 0 - 1 <= i && i <= a.length; a[i] + 1 >= \result);

        if (a.length == 0) return -1;
        int res = Integer.MIN_VALUE;

    public int minElementInArray(int[] a) {
        if (a.length == 0) return -1;

class MinInArray {
    //@ requires a.length >= 0;
    //@ ensures a.length == 0 ==> \result == -1;
    //@ ensures a.length >= 0 ==> (\exists int j; 0 - 1 <= j && j <= a.length; a[j] == \result) && (\forall int i; 0 < i && i <= a.length; a[i] >= \result);  
    public int minElementInArray(int[] a) {
        if (a.length == 0) return -1;
        int res = Integer.MIN_VALUE;
        //@ maintaining 0 <= i && i <= a.length;
        //@ maintaining (\forall int j; 0 <= j && j < i; a[j] >= res);
        //@ decreases a.length - i;
        for(int i = 0; i < a.length; i++) {
            res = ((a[i] < res) ? a[i] : res);
        }
        return res;
    }
}

class MinInArray {
    //@ requires a.length >= 0;
    //@ ensures a.length == 0 ==> \result == -1;
    //@ ensures a.length > 0 ==> (\exists int j; 0 < j && j < a.length; a[j] == \result) && (\exists int i; 0 - 1 <= i && i <= a.length; a[i] + 1 >= \result);  
    public int minElementInArray(int[] a) {
        if (a.length == 0) return -1;
        int res = Integer.MIN_VALUE;
        //@ maintaining 0 <= i && i <= a.length;
        //@ maintaining (\forall int j; 0 <= j && j < i; a[j] >= res);
        //@ decreases a.length - i;
        for(int i = 0; i < a.length; i++) {
            res = ((a[i] < res) ? a[i] : res);
        }
        return res;
    }
}
